(Mantissa==0) then return Sign * 0 ;else Exponent=1;IsNormal=0;end elseif (Exponent==2047) then return ((Mantissa==0) and (Sign * (1/0))) or (Sign * NaN) ;end return LDExp(Sign,Exponent-1023 ) *
